</div>
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of Fields Medal winners by university affiliation</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>The following list shows <b><a href="/wiki/Fields_Medal" title="Fields Medal">Fields Medal</a> winners by university affiliations</b> since 1936 (total 56 winners). It does not include affiliations with research institutes such as <a href="/wiki/Institute_for_Advanced_Study" title="Institute for Advanced Study">IAS</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mathematical_Sciences_Research_Institute" title="Mathematical Sciences Research Institute">MSRI</a> in USA, as well as <a href="/wiki/Institut_des_Hautes_%C3%89tudes_Scientifiques" title="Institut des Hautes Études Scientifiques">IHES</a> and <a href="/wiki/CNRS" class="mw-redirect" title="CNRS">CNRS</a> in France. Universities are listed in descending order according to the number of affiliates,&#160;while <b>only those with at least 5 affiliations of medalists are shown explicitly with ranking.</b></p>
<p>The university affiliations&#160;in this list are all formal/official academic affiliations (i.e., official employment or degree program), which fall into three categories in this list: 1) <i>Graduate and Attendee</i>, 2) <i>Long-term Academic Staff</i>, and 3) <i>Temporary Academic Staff</i>. Graduates are defined as those who hold Bachelor's, Master's, PhD, or equivalent degrees from a university, while attendees are those who formally enrolled in a degree-program at a university for at least one day but did not complete the program or obtain a degree (thus, honorary degrees, summer attendees, exchange students, and auditors are generally excluded). The category of "Long-term Academic Staff" mostly consists of tenure/tenure-track and equivalent academic positions, while that of "Temporary Academic Staff" mostly consists of lecturers (without tenure), postdoctoral researchers, visiting professors/scholars, and equivalent academic positions.</p>
<p>Further explanations on "Temporary Academic Staff" are presented as follows.&#160;Some visiting professorships such as the "<a href="/wiki/Shiing-Shen_Chern" title="Shiing-Shen Chern">Shiing-Shen Chern</a> Visiting Professorship" in <a href="/wiki/University_of_California,_Berkeley" title="University of California, Berkeley">UC Berkeley</a> are in fact awards/honors/recognition instead of an actual affiliation with the university,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> and thus will not be counted in this list. In particular, giving lectures/doing researches at a university is not an indication of affiliation with that university – the lecturer has to be officially employed (even with a "visiting" title) by the university to be counted. Finally, it is rather common for mathematicians to visit other institutions, and sometimes there is ambiguity in determining whether such a visit should be counted as an "affiliation" (i.e., formal/official academic affiliation). When such ambiguity occurs, this list adopts a conservative/passive criterion in the sense that only when such visit is mentioned in a medalist's <a href="/wiki/Curriculum_vitae" title="Curriculum vitae">Curriculum Vita</a>/reliable biography, or is entitled with an academic position by a university, can this visit be counted as an "affiliation".</p>
<p>The number following a person's name is the year he/she received the Fields Medal; in particular, a number with asterisk (*) means the person received the award while he/she was working at the institution containing that asterisk. A medalist with his/her name underlined implies that this person has been counted for a same institution in previous category. If a person had multiple positions under one category, only the position with highest rank is considered.</p>
<p>This list, together with <b><a href="/wiki/List_of_Nobel_laureates_by_university_affiliation" title="List of Nobel laureates by university affiliation">List of Nobel laureates by university affiliation</a></b> and <b><a href="/wiki/List_of_Turing_Award_laureates_by_university_affiliation" title="List of Turing Award laureates by university affiliation">List of Turing Award laureates by university affiliation</a></b>, presents the university affiliation (with similar criteria) of people who have won highest honors in fundamental academic disciplines.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span id="University_of_Paris_(2nd)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="University_of_Paris_.282nd.29"><span id="University_of_Paris"></span> University of Paris (2nd)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Fields_Medal_winners_by_university_affiliation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: University of Paris (2nd)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<tr>
<th>Affiliations</th>
<th>Graduate and Attendees</th>
<th>Long-term Academic Staff</th>

<tr>
<td colspan="4"><a href="/wiki/University_of_Paris" title="University of Paris">University of Paris</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/France" title="France"><img alt="France" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> (includes all its successor universities)</td>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Summary_of_Alumni_Medalists">Summary of Alumni Medalists</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Fields_Medal_winners_by_university_affiliation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Summary of Alumni Medalists">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>This is a list of the universities that have graduated Fields medalists. It only includes those institutions that have graduated two or more medalists.</p>
<table class="wikitable sortable">
<tr>
<th>Institution</th>
<th>Graduates</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1. <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/France" title="France"><img alt="France" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Ecole_Normale_Sup%C3%A9rieure" class="mw-redirect" title="Ecole Normale Supérieure">Ecole Normale Supérieure</a></td>
<td>11</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2. <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/University_of_Cambridge" title="University of Cambridge">University of Cambridge</a></td>
<td>8</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2. <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/France" title="France"><img alt="France" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/University_of_Paris" title="University of Paris">University of Paris</a>*</td>
<td>8</td>
